						has_country_flag = UKR_military_personnel
					}

					clear_variable = UKR_inf_war_making_bet_weekly_manpower
					clear_variable = UKR_inf_war_making_bet_command_power_gain_mult

				clr_country_flag = UKR_military_personnel
				set_country_flag = UKR_psychological_operation

					var = UKR_monthly_increase_var_add
					value = 1.5
				}
				RUS = {
					add_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = UKR_propaganda_debuff

	UKR_EM = {
		icon = GFX_UKR_VSY_defense
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = RUS
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_war_with = RUS
		}
		activation = {
			OR = {
				has_war = yes
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = UKR_EM_end
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision UKR_EM"

	UKR_buy_mgtes = {
		fire_only_once = no
		available = {
			has_completed_focus = UKR_usaid_mgtes
		}
		visible = {
			tag = UKR
			has_completed_focus = UKR_usaid_mgtes
		}
		days_remove = 7
		days_re_enable = 14
		cost = 100
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision UKR_buy_mgtes: remove_effect"
			add_to_variable = {
				energy_mobile_gas_turbine_power_plant_units = 1
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_free_mgtes_tt
		}
	}

		days_remove = 0
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = UKR_prepare_naval_invasion_in_nova_kahovka_flag
		}
		available = {
			divisions_in_state = {
				size < 5
				state = 253
			}
			num_battalions_in_states = {
				exclude = { marine }
				count > 7
				states = { 253 }
			}
			has_full_control_of_state = 253
			controls_province = 10681
			RUS = {
				has_full_control_of_state = 644
				controls_province = 18396
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			NOT = {
				divisions_in_state = {
					size < 5
					state = 253
				}
				num_battalions_in_states = {
					exclude = { marine }
					count > 7
					states = { 253 }
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_full_control_of_state = 253
				controls_province = 10681
			}
			NOT = {
				RUS = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 644
					controls_province = 18396
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = UKR_prepare_naval_invasion_in_nova_kahovka_flag
			UKR_naval_invasion_in_nova_kahovka = yes
		}
	}
